# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Kimball's Data Warehouse Architecture: Evaluating the Challenges of Conformed Data against the Inmon Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27571)
*Júlio Rocha,Salviano Soares,António Valente,Filipe Cabral Pinto*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文比较了Inmon的企业信息工厂（Hub-and-Spoke）架构与Kimball的数据总线/维度建模架构（如星型模式），并指出两者并非对立，而是互补的，Kimball更关注用户需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据快速增长，组织需要重构存储框架以高效处理查询。研究Inmon和Kimball这两种经典数据仓库架构方法，以指导架构选择。

Method: 通过对Inmon的Hub-and-Spoke架构和Kimball的数据总线/维度建模架构进行比较分析，聚焦四个关键维度：信息质量、系统质量、个人影响和组织影响。

Result: 尽管两种架构解决方案不同，但两位作者并不视对方为竞争对手，Kimball的架构更关注最终用户需求。

Conclusion: Inmon和Kimball的架构各有侧重，可根据组织需求选择或结合使用，两者并非对立关系。

Abstract: In recent decades, driven by rapid data growth, organisations have faced the need to restructure their storage frameworks to efficiently handle queries requested by employees through available enterprise applications. Investigating this need involves examining the classic approaches of William H. Inmon, widely known as the father of Data Warehousing, and Ralph Kimball. Although both shared the same core concerns, Kimball later suggested an alternative architecture focused primarily on user needs. According to Ariyachandra and Watson, Inmon's "hub-and-spoke" architecture and Kimball's data bus framework featuring conformed dimensions stand out among alternative approaches. A comparison across these architectures highlights four key aspects: Information Quality, System Quality, Individual Impacts, and Organisational Impacts. Although Kimball and Inmon proposed contrasting solutions, they did not view each other as rivals. For instance, in one of the editions of the book "The Data Warehouse Toolkit", published by Kimball in 1996, the back cover features a note by Inmon stating that it is "one of the definitive books of our industry. If you take time to read only one professional book, make it this book.

</details>


### [2] [DiStash: A Disaggregated Multi-Stash Transactional Key-Value Store](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27979)
*Yiming Gao,Hieu Nguyen,Jun Li,Shahram Ghandeharizadeh*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: DiStash是一个去中心化的事务性键值存储系统，能够跨不同存储池（如DRAM、SSD、HDD、NVM）进行统一事务管理，支持数据的复制（inclusive）或分层（exclusive）存储，并基于FoundationDB实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV存储难以跨异构存储池（如DRAM、SSD、HDD、NVM）提供事务一致性，容易出现数据副本不一致或节点故障导致的数据丢失问题，应用逻辑复杂化。

Method: 提出DiStash架构，通过扩展FoundationDB实现跨存储池的事务性KV管理；支持应用指定存储池为临时或持久存储，并选择数据包含（复制）或互斥（分层）模式。

Result: 通过微基准测试和eBay生产负载量化了设计权衡，并开源了实现代码。

Conclusion: DiStash能够简化跨异构存储池的KV管理，避免数据不一致和丢失问题，提供灵活的事务性支持。

Abstract: A stash is a storage medium such as Dynamic Random Access Memory (DRAM), Solid State Disk (SSD), Hard Disk Drive (HDD), or Non-Volatile Memory (NVM). This paper presents a disaggregated transactional key-value (KV) store, DiStash, that governs KVs cross pools of stash types. It enables an application to use a single transaction to read and write different copies of one or more key-value pair across the different pools of stashes. It simplifies the application logic by (a) preventing undesirable race conditions that may cause copies of data across different stash pools to reflect different values and/or (b) failures that may result in loss of key-value pairs. A configuration of DiStash may use a pool of stashes as either ephemeral or durable storage. The application dictates whether the content of its participating stashes are inclusive (replicated) or exclusive (tiered). We implement a DiStash by extending FoundationDB. We quantify the tradeoffs with its design decisions using microbenchmarks and eBay's production workload. We open source our implementation at https://github.com/ebay-USC/DiStash.

</details>


### [3] [Single and Multi Truth Data Fusion using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28062)
*Hira Beril Kucuk,Norman W Paton,Jiaoyan Chen,Zhenyu Wu*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文研究了使用大语言模型（LLMs）进行表格数据融合（真值发现）任务，提出了多种提示策略，实验表明LLM方法在所有数据集上均优于传统无监督真值发现方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大语言模型在数据融合（真值发现）任务中的潜力，以解决传统方法在单真值和多真值场景中处理冲突数据时的局限性。

Method: 针对表格数据，设计了多种提示策略，涵盖单真值与多真值场景、领域相关与领域无关、零样本与单样本提示，并在三个基准数据集上进行实证评估。

Result: 基于LLM的方法在所有数据集上均优于传统无监督真值发现方法（如DART和LTM）。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在数据融合任务中具有显著优势，能够有效处理单真值和多真值场景下的冲突数据，且代码已开源。

Abstract: Data fusion, also known as truth discovery, is a data integration problem that aims to determine the correct value or set of values for each attribute of an object when presented with potentially conflicting values from multiple sources. Data fusion tasks belong to two main categories: single-truth scenarios, where each attribute has only one correct value, and multi-truth scenarios, where multiple values can be valid simultaneously. This paper investigates the use of Large Language Models (LLMs) in data fusion tasks for tabular data. Various prompting strategies, encompassing both single-truth and multi-truth scenarios, are investigated empirically. Domain-dependent, domain-independent, zero-shot and one-shot prompts are evaluated on three different benchmark datasets. Experimental results demonstrate that LLM-based approaches outperform traditional unsupervised truth discovery methods, such as DART and LTM, across all datasets. The codebase of this study has been made publicly available on GitHub.

</details>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [How far does a random forest generalize from a 54-run LAMMPS+SPICA benchmark?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27695)
*Dennis Alves Pedersen,Paulo Henrique Leme Ramalho,Fábio Andrijauskas*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出使用冷启动随机森林代理模型（基于54次LAMMPS+SPICA运行数据）预测混合MPI+OpenMP配置的分子动力学性能，在单节点/多节点/共享线程等架构边界内可正确排序配置，为减少基准测试开销提供了可信任的推荐范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上为分子动力学负载选择近优的MPI+OpenMP混合配置需要大量穷举基准测试，消耗大量分配预算。作者希望探索能否通过一次性训练的小规模结构化基准数据集构建代理模型，可靠预测性能并推荐高配置，从而避免反复集群运行。

Method: 基于54次LAMMPS+SPICA运行（抗菌肽Tritrpticin在水化DOPC双层上的粗粒度模拟）构建训练集，涵盖1-8个AMD EPYC 7662节点上的18种混合配置（3次重复）。提取9个拓扑与资源特征，训练5种回归器预测循环时间及4个LAMMPS内部时序分数（Pair, Kspace, Comm, Modify）。采用留一维度外推广评估泛化能力。

Result: 样本内平均绝对误差为0.49秒（相对误差4.0%）。特征重要性显示预测信号集中在拓扑变量（OpenMP线程数和MPI/OpenMP比率占主导，原始节点数和核心数贡献不足3%）。留一维度外泛化表明准确性受硬件体制成员关系控制：在单一体制内（单节点、多节点或共享线程层级）代理模型能正确排序配置，跨架构边界时精度下降。

Conclusion: 得到一个可解释的信任地图，标明代理模型推荐在何处可信，有助于以名义成本的极小部分来规划进一步的基准测试活动。

Abstract: Selecting near-optimal hybrid MPI+OpenMP configurations for molecular dynamics workloads on modern HPC clusters has traditionally required exhaustive empirical benchmarking, consuming allocation budget proportional to the number of configurations evaluated. This work investigates whether a cold-start Random Forest surrogate, trained once on a small, structured benchmark dataset, can reliably predict execution performance and recommend high-performing configurations without further cluster runs. The training dataset comprises 54 LAMMPS+SPICA runs of the antimicrobial peptide Tritrpticin on a hydrated DOPC bilayer (4 354 coarse-grained beads), spanning 18 hybrid configurations on 1-8 AMD EPYC 7662 nodes of the Lovelace cluster at CENAPAD-SP, with three independent replications each. Nine topology and resource features feed five regressors that predict loop time and four internal LAMMPS timing fractions (Pair, Kspace, Comm, Modify). In-sample mean absolute error is 0.49 s on loop time (4.0 % relative). Feature importance localizes predictive signal in topology variables (OpenMP threads and MPI/OpenMP ratio dominate; raw node and core counts contribute under 3 %). Leave-one-dimension-out generalization reveals that accuracy is governed by hardware regime membership: within a common regime (single-node, multi-node, or shared threading tier) the surrogate ranks configurations correctly, and degrades when targets cross architectural boundaries. The result is an interpretable map of where the surrogate's recommendations can be trusted, useful for scoping further benchmark campaigns at a fraction of their nominal cost.

</details>


### [5] [Lightweight Multi-Vehicle Collaborative Perception Acceleration with Fusion Position Adjustment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27750)
*Wenzhao Zhang,Shujun Han,Haixiao Gao,Mengying Sun,Bizhu Wang,Xiaodong Xu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文针对多车协同感知中的轻量化加速问题，提出了一种基于线性层前向/后向特征融合位置调整的无精度损失加速方案FALL，在有限计算和通信资源下可分别降低高达30.3%和74.8%的延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多车协同感知是自动驾驶的关键技术，但实时MvCP在有限资源下运行面临挑战，现有方法难以兼顾计算和通信资源的限制。

Method: 定义了条件可加性概念并分析DNN线性层的条件可加性，针对基于加性特征融合的IF-MvCP，推导了线性层间特征融合位置调整的前向/后向精度一致性，提出FALL方案（线性层间特征融合位置调整），实现理论上无精度损失的加速。

Result: 实验验证了特征融合位置调整的精度一致性；FALL方案在有限通信资源下最多降低74.8%延迟，在有限计算资源下最多降低30.3%延迟。

Conclusion: FALL方案能有效适应计算和通信资源受限的场景，在不损失精度的前提下显著降低MvCP延迟，为实时协同感知提供了轻量化加速方案。

Abstract: Multi-vehicle collaborative perception (MvCP) is considered as a key technology to facilitate automated driving (AD), where real-time MvCP under limited resources is significant for reliable AD. In this paper, we formulate a lightweight acceleration scheme for intermediate-fusion (IF) MvCP, which can adapt to both situations of limited computation and communication resources. We provide a relaxed definition conditional additivity and analyze the conditional additivity for various DNN linear layers. On this basis, we focus on the IF-MvCP based on additive feature fusion, and derive the MvCP precision consistency of the forward and backward feature fusion position (FP) adjustments among linear layers. Through experiments, we further validate the precision consistency of the FP adjustment method. Moreover, we propose an FP adjustment among linear layers (FALL) scheme for MvCP acceleration without precision loss theoretically. Simulation results show that the proposed FALL can reduce MvCP latency by up to 74.8% under limited communication resources and by up to 30.3% under limited computation resources.

</details>


### [6] [Optimizing Teacher-Student Partitioning for Scalable Knowledge Distillation on HPC Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27797)
*Adrian P. Dieguez,Victor Conchello Vendrell,Alex Batlle,Vinnam Kim,Jordi Ros-Giralt,Harris Teague*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种HPC感知的知识蒸馏方法，通过解耦教师和学生模型的分区策略，利用两者在内存和通信上的不对称性，实现了比TRL库高达67%的样本处理速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KD框架（如TRL）对称地处理教师和学生模型，忽略了它们在内存占用和通信需求上的显著不对称性，导致效率低下。

Method: 提出HPC感知的KD方法，将教师和学生模型的分区解耦，结合垂直和水平分区策略，并通过解析表达式识别分区机制之间的拐点。

Result: 相比TRL，该方法实现了高达67%的样本处理速度提升（samples-per-second）。

Conclusion: 利用教师-学生不对称性进行拓扑感知的并行化可以显著加速知识蒸馏训练，在实际生产HPC集群上验证了有效性。

Abstract: Knowledge Distillation (KD) enables training smaller student models under the guidance of larger teacher models, and the widely adopted TRL library implements it. Yet, TRL treats both models symmetrically, missing opportunities to exploit their pronounced asymmetry in memory footprint, and communication requirements. This paper presents an HPC-aware methodology for KD that decouples teacher and student partitioning efficiently. Our approach achieves up to 67% higher samples-per-second than TRL by avoiding unnecessary teacher-model data structures and selecting the best split strategy. We combine vertical and horizontal partitioning of models, deriving an analytical expression that identifies the existence of inflection points between splitting regimes. These results showed that exploiting teacher--student asymmetry through topology-aware parallelism notably accelerated GKD training on production HPC clusters at our company

</details>


### [7] [RAMSES: Secure high-performance computing for sensitive data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27919)
*Peter Heger,Lech Nieroda,Roland Pabel,Christoph Stollwerk,Stefan Borowski,Kamil Tokmakov,Michael Commer,Martin Peifer,Stefan Wesner,Viktor Achter*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: RAMSES是一款从零开始设计的兼顾高性能与强安全的HPC系统，通过硬件内存加密、文件加密、操作系统加固和多因素认证等技术，在生物医学等敏感数据领域实现了数据全生命周期的持续加密，同时将安全措施对性能的影响控制在有限范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统HPC追求速度，安全系统牺牲速度换安全，但生命科学等领域需要同时处理大规模敏感数据，亟需一种既能保证高性能又不牺牲安全性的计算平台。

Method: 集成AMD处理器硬件内存加密、IBM Storage Scale和Thales CipherTrust管理器的高级文件加密，实现数据静止、传输和使用中的持续加密；同时实施操作系统加固、多层安全架构和强制多因素认证。

Result: 生物医学领域基准测试表明，安全环境对性能的影响有限，证明速度与安全这两个冲突的需求可以整合，同时保持系统的连贯性、灵活性和用户友好性。

Conclusion: RAMSES成功证明了高性能与高安全并非不可兼得，为需要处理敏感数据的大规模科学计算提供了一个可行的、符合多项数据保护标准的平台方案。

Abstract: Traditionally, the architecture of high-performance computing (HPC) systems is tailored for speed, while highly secure computer systems must sacrifice speed for security. However, a wide range of scientific domains, such as the life sciences, call for a combination of performance and security to allow processing sensitive data at scale. Here, we present RAMSES (Research Accelerator for Modeling and Simulation with Enhanced Security), an HPC system designed from the ground up to deliver high performance within a robust security framework. RAMSES integrates hardware-based memory encryption of AMD processors with state-of-the-art file encryption from IBM Storage Scale and the Thales CipherTrust manager, establishing an HPC platform that ensures continuous encryption throughout the data life cycle - at rest, in transit, and in use - in compliance with major data protection standards (European General Data Protection Regulation, ISO/IEC 27001 certification, and Federal Information Processing Standards). In addition, we implemented advanced operating system hardening, a multi-layered security architecture, and mandatory multi-factor authentication to adapt the HPC environment to increased security demands. Benchmark results from the biomedical sector demonstrate that the performance impact of the secure environment is limited and that integration of the conflicting requirements speed and security can be achieved while preserving a coherent, flexible, and user-friendly system.

</details>

# cs.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Incremental Dominating Set](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27469)
*Ilan Doron Arad,Jonathan Gal,Seffi Naor*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了在线增量支配集问题，提出了确定性O(Δ)竞争比算法和随机化O(log²Δ)竞争比算法，并将其扩展到连通支配集问题，同时给出了匹配的下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统在线支配集问题中，与全知离线最优解对比会导致极强下界（如星图表明竞争比至少Ω(Δ)）。为了进行更有意义的比较，作者引入了增量设置，其中在线算法和最优算法面临相同的限制。

Method: 1) 提出增量支配集模型，约束最优解与在线算法享有相同信息；2) 给出确定性O(Δ)竞争比算法和随机化O(log²Δ)竞争比算法；3) 利用线性规划（LP）将结果扩展到连通支配集问题；4) 考虑顶点带权图和提前知晓邻居信息等变体。

Result: 1) 增量支配集：确定性O(Δ)竞争比，随机化O(log²Δ)竞争比；2) 连通支配集：类似结果；3) 提前知晓邻居信息时，确定性算法可达多对数竞争比；4) 证明了匹配的下界，说明结果在常数因子内最优。

Conclusion: 增量支配集模型提供了比传统在线模型更有意义的基准，本文的结果在顶点加权图和随机化算法方面填补了空白，且最优性得到下界验证。

Abstract: Dominating Set is a fundamental problem in graph theory: given a graph, find a minimum-weight subset of vertices such that every vertex is either selected or adjacent to a selected vertex. In online settings where vertices arrive sequentially, comparing algorithms against an offline optimum with full knowledge of the input leads to extremely strong lower bounds, where even a simple star graph shows that any online algorithm must have competitive ratio $Ω(Δ)$, with $Δ$ the largest degree of any vertex in the graph, matching the trivial strategy of selecting all vertices.
  We study the incremental dominating set problem, where the optimal algorithm is constrained to the same choices available to online algorithms. This introduces a benchmark that enables a meaningful comparison between algorithms.
  We present the first results for vertex-weighted graphs and randomized algorithms in this model. For incremental dominating set, we give an $O(Δ)$-competitive deterministic algorithm and an $O(\log^2Δ)$-competitive randomized algorithm. We extend these results to the Connected Dominating Set problem using a linear-programming formulation that captures connectivity through local constraints. When the neighborhood of each arriving vertex is known \textit{in advance}, deterministic algorithms achieve similar polylogarithmic competitive ratios as their randomized counterparts. Finally, we establish matching lower bounds, showing that our results are optimal up to constant factors.

</details>


### [9] [Beating Trivial Time for Tricky Triangle Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27727)
*Neha Pant,Ryan Williams*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对几个著名的三角检测问题（全边稀疏三角、稀疏单色三角、精确三角），在Word RAM模型中首次提出了超越平凡枚举算法的改进，并利用随机算法、电路复杂性和通信复杂性技术，还解决了4-环检测问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知基于流行精细粒度猜想的平凡枚举算法被证明是最优的（指数级上），但鉴于3SUM存在非平凡算法，自然好奇这些三角检测问题是否也能被改进。

Method: 综合运用随机算法、电路复杂性（多项式规模AC0操作）和通信复杂性技术，在Word RAM模型中设计新算法。

Result: 首次在Word RAM模型中对全边稀疏三角、稀疏单色三角、精确三角问题实现了优于平凡算法的改进；同时解决了n节点图上4-环检测的o(n²)时间算法；还实现了在AC0字操作下对大小为2^u的宇宙中n个元素的排序。

Conclusion: 表明即使在某些精细粒度猜想下看似最优的问题，仍可能存在非平凡改进，且AC0电路与Word RAM模型的结合能带来新的计算能力。

Abstract: For several well-studied triangle detection problems in the literature, the trivial enumeration algorithms are known to be optimal (up to the exponent) assuming popular fine-grained conjectures. For example, All-Edges Sparse Triangle and Sparse Monochromatic Triangle where each node has degree $n^δ$ for some $δ< 1$, and the Exact Triangle where edges have arbitrary weights, all have this property under the 3SUM Conjecture. However, as there are slightly nontrivial algorithms for 3SUM, it is natural to wonder if the trivial algorithm for these tricky triangle tasks might also be improved.
  Applying a variety of techniques from randomized algorithms, circuit complexity, and communication complexity, we present the first improvements over the trivial algorithms for each of these problems in the Word RAM model. Moreover, our algorithms can be implemented with only polysize $AC0$ operations on words. Extending our techniques, we also show how to solve the notorious 4-cycle detection problem on $n$-node graphs in $o(n^2)$ time, in a Word-RAM model with word size $w > ω(\log^2 n)$. Along the way, we show how to sort $n$ items over a universe of size $2^u$ using only $AC0$ word operations in $O(n u \log n)/w$ time.

</details>


### [10] [Robust Shattering Arguments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27847)
*Mohsen Ghaffari,Magnús M. Halldórsson,Yannic Maus,Alexandre Nolin*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文揭示了分布式算法中图碎裂（graph shattering）技术在超常数轮预处理阶段因依赖累积而失效的问题，指出了MIS、(Δ+1)-染色和LLL等经典算法分析中的漏洞，并提供了系统性修复方案，包括Fischer-Ghaffari LLL算法的纠正分析以及不依赖独立性的通用工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图碎裂分析依赖独立性假设来界定远距离节点未解决的概率，但超常数轮预处理中依赖会随时间累积，导致这些假设不成立，使得多个经典算法的标准碎裂论证不完整。

Method: 系统性地修复了有缺陷的碎裂分析，核心贡献是对Fischer-Ghaffari LLL算法给出了修正的碎裂分析；同时开发了捕捉现代算法通用模式的工具，能在不依赖独立性的情况下得到所需的衰减界；还给出了反例来展示常用碎裂引理的缺陷。

Result: 成功修复了MIS、(Δ+1)-染色和LLL等经典问题的标准碎裂论证，建立了在长程依赖存在下鲁棒且可复用的碎裂论证基础。

Conclusion: 图碎裂分析中常用的独立性假设在超常数轮预处理中不可靠，本文提供的系统性修复和通用工具为未来分布式算法设计提供了更坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Graph shattering is a central technique underlying sublogarithmic-time distributed algorithms in the LOCAL model. Its analysis typically relies on bounding the probability that large sets of distant nodes remain unresolved, often via independence assumptions justified by locality.
  We show that these assumptions fail for pre-shattering procedures that run for super-constant rounds, where dependencies accumulate over time. As a result, several standard shattering arguments in the literature are incomplete, including those for maximal independent set, $(Δ+1)$-coloring, and the distributed Lovász Local Lemma (LLL).
  We provide a systematic repair of these analyses. Our main contribution is a corrected shattering analysis of the Fischer--Ghaffari LLL algorithm. In addition, we develop general tools that capture common patterns in modern algorithms and yield the required decay bounds without relying on independence. We also present explicit counterexamples to commonly used shattering lemmas.
  Overall, we establish a robust and reusable foundation for shattering arguments in the presence of long-range dependencies.

</details>


### [11] [An Exponential Lower Bound for Spectral Density Estimation on Unweighted Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28188)
*Pan Peng,Yuyang Wang,Joy Qiping Yang,Yichun Yang*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明在无权图上，谱密度估计需要指数级随机游走样本量的下界，具体为 $2^{\Omega(1/\varepsilon^{1/6})}$ 次随机游走，每次长度为 $2^{\Omega(1/\varepsilon^{1/6})}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前 Cohen-Steiner 等人提出用 $2^{O(1/\varepsilon)}$ 次随机游走实现 $\varepsilon$-近似谱密度估计；Jin 等人对加权图证明了匹配的指数下界，但无权图的下界是否成立悬而未决。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 通过构造一类特殊的无权图，证明任何算法在给定有限随机游走数据（从均匀随机节点出发）的情况下，无法以高概率区分该图与参考图，从而导出谱密度估计的指数下界。

Result: 证明无权图上谱密度估计的指数下界：需要 $2^{\Omega(1/\varepsilon^{1/6})}$ 次随机游走，每次长度 $2^{\Omega(1/\varepsilon^{1/6})}$，才能以常概率实现 $\varepsilon$-近似（Wasserstein-1 距离）。

Conclusion: 回答了 Jin 等人留下的公开问题，将指数下界从加权图推广到无权图，表明即使图结构更简单，谱密度估计的样本复杂性本质上仍是指数级别的。

Abstract: We study lower bounds for estimating the spectral density of the normalized adjacency matrix of a graph. Previously, Cohen-Steiner et al. [KDD 2018] proposed an algorithm for $\varepsilon$-approximate spectral density estimation in the Wasserstein-1 distance, using $2^{O(1/\varepsilon)}$ random walks initiated from uniformly random nodes in the graph. Later, Jin et al. [COLT 2023] established a nearly matching exponential lower bound for \emph{weighted} graphs, assuming the algorithm has access to samples from random walks started at random nodes. It was left open whether this lower bound could be extended to \emph{unweighted} graphs.
  In this paper, we answer this question in the affirmative by proving an exponential lower bound for unweighted graphs. Specifically, we show that no algorithm can compute an $\varepsilon$-approximation to the spectrum of a normalized graph adjacency matrix with constant success probability, even when given the full transcripts of $2^{Ω(1/\varepsilon^{1/6})}$ random walks, each of length $2^{Ω(1/\varepsilon^{1/6})}$, started from uniformly random nodes.

</details>

### [12] [Test-Input Generation for Tensor Programs: What Actually Finds Kernel Bugs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27396)
*Dipankar Sarkar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了张量核测试输入生成的七种策略，基于26个算子语料库（16个正确控制+10个LLM风格错误变体）。边界形状采样策略表现最佳：对错误核78%召回率、控制组0%假阳性。对抗性值采样虽召回率99%但假阳性高达94%。正则策略完全无法检测softmax尾掩码错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量核的测试输入生成长期以来依赖经验做法（选取代表性形状和数据类型，运行固定形状的allclose检查），缺乏系统化的策略选择和量化评估。作者希望将隐式选择显式化，并衡量不同策略的实际效果。

Method: 使用gpuemu算子模式感知的种子模糊测试工具（arXiv:2606.20128），在RTX 3060 GPU实例上，对26个算子语料库（16个正确控制核+10个基于文献转录模式注入的LLM风格错误变体）评估七种测试生成策略。策略在形状候选集、数据类型组合和输入值分布三个维度上变化。评估指标为错误召回率和控制假阳性率。

Result: 边界形状采样：召回率78%（10个错误核），假阳性0%（16个控制核）。对抗性值采样：召回率99%，假阳性94%（因注入NaN/Inf触发验证器NaN检查）。正则策略（无边界形状）对softmax尾掩码错误召回率0%，边界形状则分别提升至100%和62%。

Conclusion: 边界形状采样是实际操作中最安全的策略，在保持高召回率的同时不产生误报。研究揭示了不同策略捕获的错误模式差异，强调结果阐释应关注策略对特定注入错误模式的覆盖能力，而非任何特定LLM的错误率。

Abstract: Test-input generation for tensor kernels is folkloric. Most projects pick a representative shape and dtype, run a fixed-shape allclose-style check, and ship. We make the choices explicit and measure them. Using the gpuemu op-schema-aware seeded fuzzer (arXiv:2606.20128), we evaluate seven test-generation strategies across a 26-op corpus (16 correct controls and 10 LLM-style buggy variants seeded with documented transcription patterns) on an RTX 3060 GPU instance. Strategies vary the shape candidate set, the dtype mix, and the input value distribution. We report each strategy on two axes: bug recall and control false-positive (FP) rate. Boundary-only shape sampling is the operationally safe winner: 78% recall on the 10 buggy kernels with 0% FP on the 16 controls. Adversarial value sampling reaches higher recall (99%) but inflates control FP to 94% because the strategy injects NaN and Inf inputs and the validator's NaN check fires on every kernel that propagates them, not only on buggy kernels. On the two softmax tail-mask bugs the "regular" strategy (no boundary shapes) catches 0%, while boundary raises recall to 100% and 62% respectively. That gap is the clearest single signal in the data. The corpus result is about which seeded bug patterns each strategy catches, not about the bug rate of any specific deployed LLM.

</details>


### [13] [Implementing GenAI-Supported Learning in Software Engineering and Computer Science Education using Bloom's Taxonomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27398)
*Vahid Garousi,Zafar Jafarov,Aytan Mövsümova,Leyla Memmedova,Hüseyn Mirzayev*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于布鲁姆分类法的显性教学指导框架，用以规范生成式AI在软件工程/计算机科学教育中的使用。研究发现学生认为AI在分析、评估等高层认知活动中最有价值，而明确的层级指导能促进学生反思性使用AI。研究结论强调，AI的教育价值在于认知目标、教学指导与学习者自我调节的 intentional 对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在软件工程教育中的普及带来了学习支持机遇，但也引发了浅层学习和学术诚信方面的担忧。现有研究缺乏如何通过教学指导来规范学生合理使用AI的实证探索。本文旨在探究基于布鲁姆分类法的显性教学指导如何促进AI在SE/CS教育中的负责任使用，并了解师生对AI辅助学习的看法。

Method: 研究设计了一个布鲁姆对齐的GenAI框架，明确规定了AI在不同认知层级中的适当角色。该框架被嵌入到贝尔法斯特女王大学和阿塞拜疆技术大学多门SE/CS课程的指令、实验和评估中。数据通过匿名问卷和学习工件收集，采用主题分析法，以布鲁姆分类法作为分析透镜。

Result: 学生认为GenAI在高层认知活动（分析、评估、反思）中最有价值，而在基础学习层面不太适用。明确的布鲁姆层级指导促使学生反思性地使用AI，在需要独立思考时，学生会延迟使用或有意不使用。师生均报告了教学收益，同时也面临认知努力和教学设计工作量方面的挑战。

Conclusion: 生成式AI的教育价值在于认知学习目标、教学指导与学习者自我调节三者的有意对齐。布鲁姆分类法为SE/CS教育中负责任的GenAI使用提供了一个可扩展的、以教学法驱动的框架，是强制执行式应对方案的一个实用替代方案。

Abstract: Context: Generative AI adoption in software engineering education raises opportunities for learning support alongside concerns about superficial learning and academic integrity.
  Objective: This study investigates how explicit instructional guidance aligned with Bloom's taxonomy supports responsible GenAI use in SE/CS education, exploring student and instructor perceptions of GenAI-supported learning.
  Method: We designed a Bloom-aligned GenAI framework that articulated appropriate GenAI roles at different cognitive levels. The framework was embedded in course instructions, labs, and assessment across multiple SE/CS courses at Queen's University Belfast and Azerbaijan Technical University. Data were collected via anonymous questionnaires and learning artifacts, analyzed using thematic analysis with Bloom's taxonomy as an analytic lens.
  Results: Students perceived GenAI as most valuable for higher-order cognitive activities (analysis, evaluation, reflection) and less suitable for foundational learning. Explicit Bloom-level guidance influenced students to use GenAI reflectively, with delayed or intentional non-use when independent thinking was prioritized. Both students and instructors reported pedagogical benefits alongside challenges in cognitive effort and instructional design workload.
  Conclusion: GenAI's educational value lies in intentional alignment between cognitive learning goals, instructional guidance, and learner self-regulation. Bloom's taxonomy provides a scalable, pedagogy-driven framework for responsible GenAI use in SE/CS education, offering a practical alternative to enforcement-focused responses.

</details>


### [14] [Formal Grammars in Business Process Management: A Systematic Literature Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27399)
*Milliam Maxime Zekeng Ndadji*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了34篇关于形式文法与业务流程管理（BPM）交叉研究的主要文献，识别出七个研究流，并指出各流之间缺乏综合，呼吁更统一地利用文法理论推动BPM发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式文法在BPM领域已展现出独特的生成、声明式和分析能力，但相关研究分散在多个方向，缺乏系统性的梳理与整合，阻碍了文法理论在BPM中的深度应用。

Method: 采用系统文献综述方法，筛选出34篇主要研究，识别并归类为七个研究流，对每个流的贡献、所用形式化方法和局限性进行综合，并归纳出五个基于语料库的开放挑战。

Result: 发现了七个研究流：①组织流程设计的过程文法；②基于BWW本体框架评估流程建模语言；③流程结构规范与变体管理的产生式规则文法；④工作流声明式规范与分布式执行的属性文法；⑤流程模型转换、生成与语义分析的图文法；⑥流程挖掘与发现的文法推断；⑦行为规范与验证的进程代数。各流发展平行，缺乏交叉综合。

Conclusion: 形式文法已影响BPM全生命周期，但七个研究流彼此孤立。论文指出，更深层次、统一地利用文法理论有望显著推动BPM领域发展。

Abstract: Business Process Management (BPM) is concerned with the systematic design, execution, monitoring, and improvement of business processes. Formal grammars have emerged as a particularly fruitful formalism for BPM, offering generative, declarative, and analytical capabilities that are uniquely well-suited to process-oriented concerns. This paper presents a systematic literature review of 34 primary studies at the intersection of formal grammars and BPM. We identify seven research streams: (i) process grammars for organizational process design; (ii) process modeling languages evaluated as grammars under the Bunge-Wand-Weber ontological framework; (iii) production-rule grammars for process structural specification and variant management; (iv) attribute grammars for the declarative specification and distributed execution of workflows; (v) graph grammars for the transformation, generation, and semantic analysis of process models; (vi) grammatical inference for process mining and discovery; and (vii) process algebras as grammar-like compositional frameworks for behavioral specification and verification. For each stream, we synthesize contributions, formalisms employed, and limitations. The review reveals that formal grammars have influenced BPM across every lifecycle phase (from organizational design to formal verification and data-driven discovery) yet the seven streams have developed largely in parallel, without cross-stream synthesis. We identify five corpus-grounded open challenges and argue that a deeper, unified exploitation of grammatical theory holds significant promise for advancing the state of the art in BPM.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语义代码搜索和克隆检测对软件开发、维护和重用至关重要，而当前深度学习模型在超大规模代码库（TB级）上的第一阶段召回表现尚不清楚，需要系统评估其有效性、效率和可扩展性。

Method: 在多语言、多数据集上对当代深度学习模型进行基准测试；提出基于LLM的代码标准化（code normalisation）和查询重写（query-rewriting）方案。

Result: 现有模型在TB级源码集合上存在精度和可扩展性的关键限制；提出的LLM方案能显著提升低性能模型的精度。

### [16] [Towards Evaluation of Implicit Software World Models in Coding LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27406)

Method: 以SWE-bench Verified为数据源，让模型预测峰值内存、壁钟时间及方法级/行级性能分析排名结果，同时评估测试结果和异常类别。

Result: 所有测试模型（包括前沿模型）表现都有限且行为脆弱，预测准确率不高。

In this paper, we take a step toward a broader evaluation by shifting the observable axis to execution resources: alongside test outcome and exception class, we predict peak memory, wall-clock time, and ranked profiler outputs at method and line granularity. We use SWE-bench Verified as the source of data to hold the test close to real-world software engineering tasks. All tested models, frontier ones included, show modest performance and brittle behaviour, suggesting a notable lack of understanding of how software is executed, as opposed to how its source code is written.

### [17] [Speculative Refinement: A Hybrid Autoregressive Diffusion Decoding Strategy and Its Behavior Across Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27474)
*Aditi Gupta,Neel Mishra,Kushagra Trivedi,Pawan Kumar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过Speculative Refinement（一种无需训练的混合解码方法），系统研究了结合自回归（AR）与扩散解码的生成系统的评估问题。在六个基准测试和三种评估协议下，发现了四个关键发现：代码基准混淆了结构发现与逻辑正确性、多阶段修正会恶化已正确token导致基准饱和天花板、似然度评估与生成式评估产生不同模型排名、标准Python后处理会破坏非AR生成器的代码评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前缺乏对结合自回归和扩散解码的混合生成系统的评估方法研究，需要系统性地理解如何正确评估这类多阶段或非自回归生成管道。

Method: 提出Speculative Refinement（SpecRef）方法，这是一种无需训练的混合解码方法，通过熵引导的选择性掩码，从AR草稿中热启动掩码扩散语言模型。在六个基准测试（HumanEval、MBPP、GSM8K、BBH、ARC-Challenge、HellaSwag）上，使用三种评估协议（基于执行的pass@1、精确匹配、对数似然评分）进行评估。

Result: (1) 代码基准将结构发现与逻辑正确性混淆：仅提供语法脚手架就能使准确率从接近零提升到20%以上；(2) 多阶段修正会恶化已正确token，暴露出单模型评估无法察觉的基准饱和天花板；(3) 对数似然评估与生成式评估对同一模型对产生不同的排名；(4) 标准Python后处理会非AR生成器的代码评估产生静默破坏。

Conclusion: 这些发现适用于任何多阶段或非自回归生成管道，指向更具诊断性的评估实践。

Abstract: How should we evaluate generation systems that combine autoregressive (AR) and diffusion decoding? We study this question through Speculative Refinement (SpecRef), a training-free hybrid method that warm-starts a masked diffusion language model from an AR draft using entropy-guided selective masking. Evaluating SpecRef across six benchmarks (HumanEval, MBPP, GSM8K, BBH, ARC-Challenge, HellaSwag) with three distinct evaluation protocols (execution-based pass@1, exact-match, log-likelihood scoring), we surface several findings relevant beyond our specific system: (1) code benchmarks conflate structural discovery with logical correctness: providing a syntactic scaffold lifts accuracy from near zero to over 20% without changing the model, indicating that much of the baseline failure is structural; (2) a refinement tension phenomenon where multi-stage correction degrades already-correct tokens, exposing benchmark saturation ceilings invisible to single-model evaluation; (3) log-likelihood and generative evaluation produce different model rankings for the same model pair, suggesting they measure different capabilities; (4) standard Python post-processing silently breaks code evaluation for non-AR generators. These observations apply to any multi-stage or non-autoregressive generation pipeline and point toward more diagnostic evaluation practices.

</details>


### [18] [Contextual Associations Between Webpage Elements for Web Accessibility: An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27506)
*Kishan Rakesh,Shiyi Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究如何从网页无障碍树中恢复元素间的上下文关联，以解决屏幕阅读器用户遇到孤立可访问名称（如"Read more"）的问题。通过构建人工标注数据集并比较四种机器学习模型与两种启发式基线，探索链接预测方法是否能跨网站泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 屏幕阅读器用户在按元素列表浏览网页时，常遇到如"Read more"这类在无障碍规范下有效但在上下文中无法理解的名称。虽然页面上存在使这些名称有意义的周围元素，但缺少将它们关联到目标的机制。目前尚无实证研究探讨如何选择与目标上下文相关的周围元素。

Method: 在35个网站（按Tranco top-million分层抽样）上构建人工标注的上下文关联数据集，每页由三名独立标注者标注。将每个页面表示为从无障碍树导出的图，并加入DOM和CSS的空间与语义特征。比较MLP、GCN、GAT和SEAL四种机器学习模型与两种启发式基线，采用留一网站交叉验证和预注册统计框架，使用Hit@K和MRR评估。

Result: 五网站作者标注预实验建立了流程并参数化了功效模拟。四种学习模型的预实验Hit@10范围为0.16–0.85，两种启发式基线为0.08–0.30。最终结果将在完整实验和分析后报告。

Conclusion: 本研究贡献了：网页上下文关联的人工标注数据集、基于无障碍树图进行链接预测以选择上下文的实证评估、以及跨网站泛化分析。

Abstract: [Context] Screen reader users navigating webpages by element list often encounter accessible names such as "Read more" that are valid under the W3C Accessible Name and Description Computation specification but uninterpretable in isolation. The surrounding elements that would make these names meaningful exist in the page but are not linked to the target by any mechanism. No prior work has empirically studied how to select which surrounding elements are contextually relevant to a given target. [Objective] This registered report investigates whether human-perceived contextual associations between webpage elements can be recovered from the accessibility tree using link prediction, and whether the learned associations generalize across websites. [Method] We will construct a dataset of human-annotated contextual associations on 35 websites, stratified across the Tranco top-million list, with three independent annotators per page. Each page is represented as a graph derived from its accessibility tree, augmented with spatial and semantic features from the DOM and CSS. We compare four machine learning models (MLP, GCN, GAT, and SEAL) against two heuristic baselines under leave-one-site-out cross-validation with a pre-registered statistical framework, using Hit@K and MRR. [Results] We have conducted a five-site author-annotated pilot study to establish the pipelines and parameterize the power simulation, with pilot Hit@10 ranging from 0.16 to 0.85 across four learned models and 0.08 to 0.30 across two heuristic baselines. The final results will be reported after the planned experiments and analyses are completed. [Conclusion] The study contributes a human-annotated dataset of contextual associations on webpages, an empirical evaluation of link prediction for context selection on accessibility-tree graphs, and a cross-site generalization analysis.

</details>


### [19] [Test Case Selection for Deep Neural Networks: A Replication Study on LLMs for Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27601)
*Ali Asgari,Mitchell Olsthoorn,Annibale Panichella*

TL;DR: 本文研究了测试用例选择（TCS）技术在LLM代码模型上的可复制性，发现基于视觉DNN的部分结论能泛化到代码LLM中，但效果因任务和模型而异：不确定性特征适合早期故障发现，表示特征适合准确率估计。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开展了大规模复制性研究，在3个代码分类任务（克隆检测、漏洞检测、技术债务预测）上，覆盖17个微调模型实例、7个预测特征和13种选择策略（含12种特征感知策略和简单随机采样基线），从准确率估计和早期故障发现两个维度进行评估。

Result: 仅有部分视觉DNN上的结论能泛化到代码LLM；不确定性特征在早期故障发现上有效，表示特征在准确率估计上更稳健；但效果在任务和模型间差异显著，说明TCS效果具有上下文依赖性。

Conclusion: 本研究为TCS技术超越视觉DNN的可复制性提供了实证证据，并为其在代码LLM操作评估中的应用提供了实践见解。

Abstract: Recently, test case selection (TCS) techniques have been explored to support the operational evaluation of deep neural networks (DNNs) under limited testing budgets, where labeling cost is a primary concern and uncovering model failures early is a key objective. Although prior studies report promising results, existing empirical evaluations focus almost exclusively on vision-based DNNs and datasets, leaving it unclear whether prior findings generalize to LLM code models. This paper presents a large-scale replication study of TCS techniques in the context of LLM code models. We re-examine established TCS strategies originally proposed for DNNs and complement them with statistical sampling strategies not previously evaluated for TCS. We assess their effectiveness on three code-related classification tasks: clone detection, vulnerability detection, and technical debt prediction. The study spans 17 task-specific fine-tuned model instances, 7 predictive features, and 13 selection strategies, including 12 feature-aware strategies and simple random sampling (SRS) as a feature-agnostic baseline. We evaluate performance along two dimensions: accuracy estimation and early failure discovery. The results indicate that only a subset of findings reported for vision-based DNNs generalize when TCS is applied to LLMs for code. In particular, uncertainty-based features are effective for early failure discovery, while representation-based features are more robust for accuracy estimation. At the same time, performance varies substantially across tasks and models, indicating that TCS effectiveness is context-dependent. Overall, this study provides empirical evidence on the replicability of TCS techniques beyond vision-based deep learning and offers insights into their use for the operational evaluation of LLMs for code.

To address this, we propose the LLMVue framework, which uses a large language model (LLM) to generate a PTG from Vue.js source code. LLMVue -guided testing also significantly improves the coverage and exploration efficiency, compared to a random exploration baseline (with the same time constraints). ### [21] [BashCoder-R1: Towards Robust and Explainable Bash Code Generation with Robustness-Aware Group Relative Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27733)
*Lei Yu,Peng Wang,Jia Xu,Jingyuan Zhang,Xin Wang,Jiajia Ma,Li Yang,Changzhi Deng,Zenghua Wang,Fengjun Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 三阶段pipeline：(1) Continual Pre-training (CPT) 领域专业化；(2) Long Chain-of-Thought SFT 进行专家验证的推理-代码对训练；(3) Robustness-Aware Group Relative Policy Optimization (R-GRPO) 强化学习，优化语法正确性、鲁棒性（shellcheck）和格式正确性的加权奖励。

Abstract: Bash scripts are the cornerstone of system administration and DevOps automation, where code quality directly impacts system stability and security. To address both, we propose BashCoder-R1, a novel framework for robust and explainable Bash script generation. Our pipeline combines: (1) Continual Pre-training (CPT) to specialize the model on Bash paradigms; (2) Long Chain-of-Thought Supervised Fine-Tuning (L-CoT SFT) on expert-validated reasoning-and-code samples to emulate proactive risk-aware thinking; and (3) Robustness-Aware Group Relative Policy Optimization (R-GRPO), a reinforcement learning phase optimizing a weighted reward for syntax correctness, robustness (via shellcheck), and format correctness. We evaluate on BashBench, a new benchmark of 952 real-world tasks (773 single-line, 179 multi-line). BashCoder-R1 achieves SyntaxPass (100.00%/94.97%), RobustWarnRate (4.01%/16.47%), RobustPass (95.99%/79.33%), FuncRate (93.01%/93.85%), and FullRate (90.04%/73.18%) for single-line/multi-line tasks, outperforming the strongest baseline DeepSeek-V3.2 (Reasoning) by 37.82% and 20.18% in FullRate. ### [22] [UNICS: Multilingual Code Search via Unified Pseudocode and Contrastive Transfer Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27747)
*Ye Fan,Jidong Ge,Chuanyi Li,Liguo Huang,Bin Luo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预训练模型在多语言代码搜索中存在数据不平衡、跨语言语义干扰、统一表示（如AST、IR）丢失关键信息等问题，且传统对比学习仅关注困难负样本，忽视了困难正样本挖掘对学习代码语义不变性的价值。

Method: 采用两阶段训练策略：第一阶段基于伪代码作为统一表示进行预训练，学习跨语言算法级逻辑；第二阶段通过多任务迁移学习，将代码分解为语义切片，结合困难正样本挖掘和跨语言动态困难负采样来适配特定语言。

Furthermore, conventional contrastive learning strategies often rely on simplistic hard negative sampling while overlooking the potential of mining hard positives to learn code's intrinsic semantic invariance. To address these challenges, we introduce UNICS, a framework for multilingual code search built on a two-stage training strategy. In the first stage, UNICS is pre-trained on a novel dataset we constructed, which uses pseudo-code as a unified representation to learn a cross-lingual, algorithm-level logic that preserves full semantic fidelity. The second stage employs a multi-task transfer learning strategy that adapts this general knowledge to specific languages by decomposing code into semantic slices (e.g., API calls, function bodies) and incorporating tasks for hard positive mining and cross-lingual dynamic hard negative sampling. Experimental results demonstrate that UNICS achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple multilingual and cross-lingual benchmarks, showcasing superior generalization and performance balance, especially in zero-shot transfer tasks to low-resource languages.

### [24] [Evolution-Aware Regression Test Prioritization of ML-Enabled Systems Using Gradient-Based Behavior Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28037)
*Eunho Cho,Donghwan Shin,In-Young Ko*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出GBV-PD方法，利用梯度行为向量空间实现演化感知的回归测试优先级排序，在不运行演化模型的情况下预测测试用例损失变化方向，优于非方向性基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ML组件通过重训练、微调和优化不断演化，导致先前有效的测试结果不再成立；单个演化步骤可能对某些测试用例提升性能而对其他用例降低性能，使得回归测试优先级排序天然具有方向性，现有方法未充分利用这一特性。

Method: 将每个测试用例表示为一个基于梯度的行为向量（GBV，损失梯度在原始模型下的低维投影），然后将演化模型的参数更新投影到相同的PCA基上，利用二者的对齐程度估计每个测试用例损失可能增加或减少的方向，无需在排序过程中运行演化模型。

Result: 在分类和回归任务上的实证研究中，GBV-PD持续优于非方向性基线方法，且与全梯度参考方法竞争力相当；在重复更新场景下，通过可重用的GBV缓存提供了更好的时间和存储效率。

Conclusion: 行为空间的思想可以被操作化为一种实用且高效的机制，用于演化中ML系统的重复更新回归测试。

Abstract: The machine learning(ML) component of an ML-enabled system evolves through retraining, fine-tuning, and optimization, so previously valid test results may no longer hold. A single evolution step can worsen performance on some test cases while improving others, making regression test prioritization inherently directional. We present Gradient-based Behavior Vector-Parameter Delta(GBV-PD), the first approach to operationalize the behavior vector space for evolution-aware regression test prioritization. GBV-PD represents each test case as a gradient-based vector(GBV), a low-dimensional projection of its loss gradient under the original model. It then projects the observed parameter update of the evolved model onto the same PCA basis and uses the resulting alignment to estimate whether each test case's loss is likely to increase or decrease, without running the evolved model on test cases during prioritization. In an empirical study across classification and regression tasks, GBV-PD consistently outperformed non-directional baselines and remained competitive with a full-gradient reference, while offering better time and storage profiles for repeated updates via reusable GBV caching. These results show that behavior-space ideas can be operationalized into a practical and efficient mechanism for repeated-update regression testing of evolving ML-enabled systems.

### [25] [SBridge: Identifying Source-to-Binary Function Similarity via Cross-Domain Control Block Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28058)

Method: 提出控制块（Control Block）概念，将函数切分为条件、循环等有意义的基本单元，以此作为跨域表示（cross-domain representation），在源码和二进制之间进行细粒度的函数相似性度量。

Abstract: We present SBridge, a precise approach for identifying functions in binaries that are similar to the given source code functions. Identifying reused code in binaries is critical for security, particularly for detecting propagated vulnerabilities. Although binary-to-binary comparison is feasible, leveraging source code as the reference is more practical because source code is easier to collect and analyze directly without compilation. However, significant gaps between source and binary representations, including function inlining, create challenges in cross-domain function detection. Existing approaches primarily rely on string literals or structural similarities between entire functions, failing to capture detailed code behavior and generating many false alarms. SBridge addresses these limitations through a key innovation: control block-based function matching, which encapsulates essential functional features by segmenting functions into meaningful units such as conditionals and loops. Leveraging control blocks as a cross-domain representation, SBridge enables precise measurement of function similarity between source and binary code, effectively overcoming challenges posed by function inlining and stripped binaries. For evaluation, we collected 3,904 real-world C/C++ binaries from BinKit. In experiments identifying binary functions identical to input source functions, despite approximately 40% of binary functions being inlined, SBridge achieved 75.13% recall@1 and 80.98% recall@5, outperforming existing approaches, which achieved up to 43.31% recall@1 and 50.2% recall@

Abstract: Context and Problem. Software development produces interrelated artifacts like software architecture documentation (SAD), software architecture models (SAMs), and source code, whose relationships are essential for maintenance and consistency checking. However, automatically recovering links between these artifacts (traceability link recovery (TLR)) remains difficult to deploy in practice. Method and Aim. We present an accessible tool landscape for ARDoCo's TLR approaches: the ARDoCo REST API exposes four TLR pipelines (SAD-SAM, SAM-Code, SAD-Code, and SAD-SAM-Code) via HTTP endpoints with asynchronous execution and caching; TraceView is a browser-based frontend with a guided wizard and interactive multi-panel exploration of recovered links and inconsistencies; and TraceViz, which is a VS Code extension that overlays trace links directly onto documentation in the IDE. Results and Conclusion. All three components are publicly deployed and usable. A preliminary study for TraceViz's in-IDE visualization confirmed that it improves developer comprehension during software understanding tasks. The tool landscape makes state-of-the-art TLR accessible to architects, developers, and tool integrators. Video. We provide a screencast of our ARDoCo Tool Landscape and how it is used here: https://youtu.be/IOTEPZQ3tVs

</details>

Abstract: Developers may reference vulnerabilities in pull request discussions through both explicit identifiers, such as CVEs or GHSAs, and implicit security-related language (e.g., "unauthorized access" or "SQL injection"). Prior work has primarily focused on explicit identifiers, potentially overlooking vulnerability discussions that lack formal references. Bots and coding agents are becoming more common in pull requests, raising new questions about how different accounts communicate about vulnerabilities. In this registered report, we describe our planned study of vulnerability communication in pull requests by humans, bots, and coding agents. Building on the AIDev-pop dataset, we analyze explicit vulnerability references and implicit security-related signals across pull request titles, descriptions, review comments, commit messages, and timeline discussions. Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的编译器测试技术仅专注于单语言编译，无法检测跨语言编译中因语义差异导致的错误，而现代JVM软件越来越多地集成多种编程语言，这类错误可能导致严重的误编译问题。

Method: 利用Kotlin编译器的统一中间表示（IR）合成跨语言测试程序，并应用7种变异算子增加测试程序的多样性，采用差分测试框架进行跨语言编译器的对比测试。

Result: 在Kotlin、Groovy、Scala 3、Scala 2和Java五个JVM编译器的最新版本中，共发现32个已确认的bug（Kotlin 15个、Groovy 4个、Scala 3 7个、Scala 2 2个、Java 4个）。

Conclusion: CrossLangFuzzer有效填补了跨语言编译器测试的空白，能够发现实际JVM编译器中的跨语言编译缺陷，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Modern JVM software increasingly integrates multiple programming languages, such as Java, Kotlin, Groovy, and Scala, within a single application. Supporting such interoperability requires JVM compilers to perform cross-language compilation while reconciling subtle semantic differences across language boundaries. Errors in this process can lead to critical miscompilations, yet existing compiler testing techniques focus exclusively on isolated, singlelanguage compilation. To address this gap, we present CrossLangFuzzer, the first differential testing framework for cross-language JVM compilation. CrossLangFuzzer leverages the Kotlin compiler's unified intermediate representation (IR) to synthesize cross-language test programs. It further applies seven mutation operators to diversify generated test programs and improve bug-finding capability. Evaluated on the latest versions of five major JVM compilers, CrossLangFuzzer uncovered 32 confirmed bugs, including 15 in Kotlin, 4 in Groovy, 7 in Scala 3, 2 in Scala 2, and 4 in Java. CrossLangFuzzer is open-source at https://github.com/XYZboom/CrossLangFuzzer

### [29] [Humanizing Automatically Generated Unit Test Suites with LLM-Based Refactoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28229)
*Wendkûuni C. Ouédraogo,Yinghua Li,Xueqi Dang,Paweł Borsukiewicz,Lingfeng Bao,Anil Koyuncu,Jacques Klein,David Lo,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: TestHumanizer 是一种混合 SBST+LLM 方法，将 LLM 作为受控重构层应用于 EvoSuite 生成的测试套件，在保持编译性和覆盖率的条件下提升可读性和可维护性，在 350 个类上达到 88-98% 编译率，开发者研究证实了显著的感知可读性和采纳意愿提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于搜索的测试生成工具（如 EvoSuite）虽然能生成高覆盖率的编译性测试，但套件可读性和可维护性差。而 LLM 直接生成更自然的测试，但编译成功率仅为 51-78%。如何结合两者优势，生成既高覆盖又易读的测试套件？

Method: 提出 TestHumanizer 混合方法：先用 EvoSuite 生成可编译、高覆盖率的测试套件，再将 LLM（gpt-4o 和 mistral-large-2407）作为受控重构层，在三种上下文配置（包括摘要设置）下对套件进行命名、结构和开发者导向清晰度的改进，同时通过验证门控确保行为与编译性保持不变。

Result: 在 350 个类（Defects4J 和 SF110）上评估：编译率达到 88-98%，接近 EvoSuite 的 100% 基线；结构覆盖率损失通常在 1-2 个百分点内；86-95% 的重构满足忠实重构阈值；预测可读性提升、控制流和认知复杂度降低、结构坏味减少。开发者研究（30 类，444 个测试方法）显示感知可读性和采纳意愿显著提升（Wilcoxon p<0.01）。概要设置提供了最稳健的权衡。

Conclusion: LLM 最有效的方式不是作为独立的生成器，而是作为经过验证门控的细化层，增强稳健的 SBST 输出。基于摘要的上下文设置提供了最佳权衡，而长代码提示更容易产生幻觉导致的失败。

Abstract: Search-based test generation tools such as EvoSuite produce compilable and high-coverage unit tests at scale, but their suites are often hard to read and maintain. LLMs can generate more natural tests, yet direct generation remains brittle, with compilation rates of only 51-78% in our study. We introduce TestHumanizer, a hybrid SBST+LLM approach that uses LLMs as controlled refactoring layers over compilable SBST suites to improve naming, structure, and developer-oriented clarity while preserving behavior and compilation validity. We evaluate TestHumanizer on 350 classes from Defects4J and SF110. EvoSuite generates 15 suites per class, and each suite is refactored under three context configurations using gpt-4o and mistral-large-2407, yielding 31,500 refactorings. TestHumanizer reaches 88-98% compilation rates, close to EvoSuite's 100% baseline and clearly above direct LLM generation. Structural coverage is largely preserved, typically within 1-2 percentage points, and 86-95% of refactorings satisfy a composite faithful-refactoring threshold. Refactored suites also improve predicted readability, reduce control-flow and cognitive complexity, and mitigate structural smells. The summary-based setting offers the most robust trade-off, while long code-centric prompts are more prone to hallucination-induced failures. A developer study on 30 classes and 444 test methods confirms significant gains in perceived readability and willingness to adopt, with Wilcoxon p less than 0.01 and substantial inter-rater agreement. Overall, LLMs are most effective not as standalone generators but as validation-gated refinement layers over robust SBST outputs.

</details>


### [30] [Govern the Repository, Not the Agent: Measuring Ecosystem-Level Risk in AI-Native Software](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28235)
*Daniel Russo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究发现，AI智能体编写的代码在整合时产生的摩擦（集成摩擦）约有一半是由仓库本身特性决定的，而非单个智能体。在相同仓库中，AI智能体贡献的代码产生的仓库级摩擦比人类贡献高出约两倍（组内相关系数0.30 vs 0.16）。问题本质上是生态系统属性，而非个体智能体属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对自主编码智能体的评估方式仍然是"一次一个智能体、在隔离的基准任务上"的传统模式，但现实是，即使每个智能体各自通过测试，共同维护的代码仓库仍会积累问题。作者想探究：这些积累的问题究竟是个体智能体的问题，还是仓库生态的问题？

Method: 分析了超过93万个由智能体编写的拉取请求（pull requests），测量"集成摩擦"（整合贡献时因并发修改产生的成本）。通过统计方法，分离出贡献者、作者、贡献大小、智能体等个体因素后，考察仓库层面能解释多少摩擦变异。同时对比了人类贡献与AI贡献的组内相关系数。

Result: 约一半的集成摩擦变异由仓库层面解释，且这一效应在完全控制其他变量后依然存在。在相同仓库中，AI智能体贡献的仓库级摩擦集中度（组内相关系数0.30）约为人类贡献（0.16）的两倍。

Conclusion: AI原生软件的风险是生态系统属性，而非个体智能体属性。因此，对AI代码的衡量和治理应从生态系统层面进行，而非一次一个智能体地评估。

Abstract: Autonomous coding agents now open and merge pull requests in shared repositories at scale, and the field evaluates them the way it has always evaluated components, one agent at a time, on isolated benchmark tasks. Yet agents that each pass their own tests still leave repositories that accumulate problems no single contribution accounts for. We ask whether this problem belongs to the individual agent or to the repository where it accumulates. We study integration friction, the cost of integrating a contribution into a codebase that other contributors are concurrently changing. Across more than 930,000 agent-authored pull requests, we measure how much of the variation in friction stays with the repository after the contribution, its author, its size, and its agent are accounted for. About half does, and it survives full controls. In the same repositories, agent-authored contributions concentrate this repository-level friction roughly twice as much as human ones (intraclass correlation 0.30 versus 0.16), a gap that holds after controlling for codebase size, age, task shape, process maturity, and merge path. The risk is a property of the ecosystem, not the agent. AI-native software is therefore better measured and governed at the ecosystem level than one agent at a time.

</details>

The deeper challenge is architectural: once AI influences how the user equipment and network interpret, predict, and adapt radio behavior, the air interface must provide common protocol semantics for coordinating such intelligence across vendors and deployments. This article presents a 3rd generation partnership project (3GPP) oriented perspective on the protocol framework for AI-native 6G air interface. We argue that standardization should preserve implementation freedom by avoiding prescription of model architectures, training methods, or model weights. Instead, 6G should define the protocol framework needed for interoperable AI operation, including how AI-enabled functions are configured, validated, activated, monitored, and safely reverted to conventional operation. ### [32] [Host-Driven Flowlet Balancing with Segment Routing over IPv6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27697)
*Ryo Nakamura,Hiroki Kano,Tomoko Okuzawa*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于SRv6的纯主机驱动的流束均衡方法，通过主机检测流束并利用SRv6进行路径选择，交换机保持无状态，实验表明相比随机流束均衡和ECMP分别降低了15%和33%的尾部延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流束均衡方法面临交换机维护每流状态的可扩展性问题，部署困难，因此需要一种交换机无需维护状态的流束均衡方案。

Method: 主机端检测出站流量中的流束，利用SRv6将流束导向特定路径；交换机作为无状态SRv6节点；引入简单模型估算每条路径上的在途字节数，以此作为负载均衡的度量指标。

Result: 在固定大小流量下，相比随机流束均衡和ECMP，尾部延迟分别降低15%和33%；结合动态调整的流束超时机制，在两种应用负载下也提升了性能。

Conclusion: 纯主机驱动的SRv6流束均衡方法在提升负载均衡性能的同时解决了交换机的状态维护瓶颈，是一种高效且可扩展的数据中心网络负载均衡方案。

Abstract: This paper proposes a fully host-driven method for flowlet balancing with Segment Routing over IPv6 (SRv6). In modern data center networks, load balancing plays a pivotal role in efficiently utilizing multiple paths. Flowlet balancing offers finer granularity in traffic splitting than ECMP and is therefore expected to achieve higher performance. However, deploying flowlet balancing in practice is still challenging due to the scalability issue of switches having to maintain per-flow state. In our approach, hosts detect flowlets in their outgoing traffic and steer them onto specific paths using SRv6. The switches behave as SRv6 nodes in a stateless manner. Each host distributes its flowlets as evenly as possible across paths. As a metric for this load balancing, we introduce a simple model that estimates in-flight bytes on each path. We implemented the proposed method on Linux and evaluated it on a testbed with an SRv6-capable router. The results show that, under fixed-size flows, the proposed method reduces tail latency by 15% and 33% compared with random flowlet balancing and ECMP, respectively. Furthermore, combining the method with dynamically adjusted flowlet timeouts also improves performance under two application workloads.

### [33] [AB-Sync: Attention-Based Slot-Level Clock Synchronization Method for UWB-TDOA Localization Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28087)
*Tianyi Lyu,Kefei Tian,Kangqiao Qin,Qingwen Liu,Mingqing Liu*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出AB-Sync，一种基于注意力机制的时隙级时钟同步方法，解决了UWB-TDOA定位网络中现有无线时钟同步方法的粒度不匹配问题，在不增加额外同步开销的情况下提升了定位精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UWB-TDOA定位网络依赖纳秒级时钟同步，但现有WCS方法仅在同步阶段或间隔级别估计时钟状态，而TDMA系统在离散短时隙中定位标签，这种粒度不匹配导致残余TDOA误差。

Method: 提出AB-Sync，利用注意力机制建模目标标签时隙特定时钟速度比与相邻时钟波动观测之间的关系，实现标签时隙级时间戳映射，无需额外UWB同步消息。

Result: 在真实UWB-TDOA测试平台上，AB-Sync相比基线方法Deferred+3S-KF，多锚点平均TDOA测距标准差降低9.4%，静态定位精度提升18.6%；在多标签实验中，各时隙定位稳定性标准差平均降低5.3%，最高达16.2%。

Conclusion: AB-Sync通过时隙级细粒度时钟同步有效提升了UWB-TDOA定位精度，且不引入额外通信开销，验证了注意力机制在解决时钟同步粒度不匹配问题上的有效性。

Abstract: Ultra-wideband (UWB) time-difference-of-arrival (TDOA) localization networks provide high-update-rate indoor location services for IoT and cyber-physical applications, but their accuracy depends on nanosecond-level clock synchronization among anchors. Existing wireless clock synchronization (WCS) methods typically estimate clock states at the synchronization-stage or interval level, whereas TDMA-based UWB-TDOA systems localize tags from blinks transmitted in discrete short slots inside each synchronization stage. We identify this granularity mismatch as a source of residual TDOA error and present AB-Sync, an attention-based slot-level clock synchronization method. AB-Sync models the relationship between the slot-specific clock-speed ratio required by a target tag blink and neighboring clock-fluctuation observations, thereby enabling tag-slot-level timestamp mapping without adding extra UWB synchronization messages. On a real UWB-TDOA testbed, AB-Sync reduces the multi-anchor average TDOA ranging STD.V by 9.4% and improves representative static localization accuracy by 18.6% compared with Deferred+3S-KF, the leading low-overhead baseline in our evaluation. In a five-slot multi-tag experiment, AB-Sync consistently improves localization stability across all TDMA slots, reducing STD.V by 5.3% on average and up to 16.2% per slot with no extra UWB synchronization overhead.

### [34] [V-TSN: A Software-Defined TSN Overlay for General-Purpose Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28285)
*Mohammadparsa Karimi,Majid Nabi,Ahmed Khalaf,Andrew Nelson,Kees Goossens,Twan Basten*

Main category: cs.NI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TSN在工业自动化、车载网络等领域至关重要，但专用TSN硬件成本高、获取困难，导致开发阶段离线仿真无法实时运行应用软件，部署阶段通用网络缺乏原生TSN支持。

Method: V-TSN通过软件定义覆盖网络的方式，在通用网络上实现gPTP时间同步与TSN流量整形（包括虚拟时间感知整形器TAS和虚拟信用整形器CBS），无需专用硬件，与未修改的应用栈实时并行运行。

Result: 在云部署中，平均时钟偏移低于200微秒；实现了对时间关键流量的虚拟TAS隔离；通过虚拟CBS实现了每类带宽预留。

Conclusion: V-TSN可作为开发阶段的仿真工具和部署阶段的经济高效选项（在宽松定时约束可接受的情况下），在通用非确定性网络上有效提供类TSN行为。

Abstract: Time-Sensitive Networking (TSN) extends Ethernet with deterministic communication for time-critical applications such as industrial automation, in-vehicle networks, and cyber-physical systems. However, realizing TSN behavior without dedicated hardware is difficult. During design and validation, offline simulation cannot run application software at real-time speed when costly specialized TSN hardware is not (yet) available. At deployment time, many systems run on general-purpose and cloud networks with no native TSN support, where provisioning full TSN hardware is unnecessary or impractical for applications that tolerate relaxed timing. In this paper, we introduce Virtual Time-Sensitive Networking (V-TSN), a software-defined overlay that realizes gPTP-based synchronization and TSN traffic shaping over general-purpose, non-deterministic networks without specialized hardware. V-TSN runs in real time alongside the unmodified application stack, serving both as a development-time emulation tool and as a cost-efficient deployment option where relaxed timing is acceptable. In a cloud-based deployment, V-TSN achieves an average clock offset below 200 microseconds, it isolates time-critical traffic through a virtual Time-Aware Shaper (TAS), and it enforces per-class bandwidth reservations through a virtual Credit-Based Shaper (CBS).

### [35] [OverFlowLight: Real-Time Gridlock Prevention and Traffic Signal Optimization for Urban Intersections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27381)
*Mingyuan Li,Boyang Huang,Tianqi Jiang,Chenpu Li,Chunyu Liu,Yang Li,Ruimin Li,Qiang Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OverFlowLight是一个基于多模态感知（相机+雷达）的实时交通信号控制框架，通过动态插入专用清空相位来预防交叉口队列溢出。在实际43个交叉口部署后，减少了60.4%的溢出事件，网络吞吐量提升18.2%，且能与现有RL信号控制智能体无缝集成。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有交通信号控制算法主要优化吞吐量，难以应对高峰时段的队列溢出问题，导致级联性交通瘫痪和安全隐患。

Method: 1) 利用相机和雷达多模态传感实现实时溢出检测；2) 动态生成并插入专用溢出清空相位；3) 混合控制设计：基于规则的快速溢出干预 + RL等后端控制器用于长期效率优化。

Result: 在三大城市43个交叉口部署：溢出事件减少60.4%，网络吞吐量提升18.2%，显著降低人工干预需求，且与现有RL信号控制智能体兼容。

Conclusion: 这是首个实际可扩展、数据驱动的主动预防交通死锁框架，为构建韧性高效的城市交通系统提供了关键组件。

Abstract: Queue overflow, a severe consequence of urban traffic congestion, occurs when vehicle queues exceed intersection capacity, obstructing upstream traffic and triggering cascading gridlocks. Prevailing traffic signal control (TSC) algorithms, primarily optimized for throughput, often fail to address overflow during peak hours, exacerbating congestion and creating safety hazards. We propose OverFlowLight, a real-time framework designed to preemptively resolve overflow and enhance overall TSC performance. It first introduces a mechanism to accurately detect overflow in real-time by leveraging multi-modal sensing from cameras and radars. Upon detection, it dynamically generates and inserts dedicated overflow phases into the signal cycle to clear the blocking queues. This is orchestrated by a hybrid control design that combines rapid rule-based overflow intervention with controller back ends such as reinforcement learning (RL) for longer-horizon efficiency. We conducted extensive real-world deployments of OverFlowLight across 43 intersections in three major cities. The framework demonstrates seamless integration with existing RL-based TSC agents, highlighting its modularity and practical applicability. Empirical results show that OverFlowLight reduces overflow incidents by 60.4% and increases network throughput by 18.2% compared to deployed baselines. Furthermore, it substantially diminishes the need for manual intervention common with expert-tuned signal plans. This work presents the first practical, scalable, and data-driven framework for actively preventing traffic gridlock, offering a crucial component for building resilient and efficient urban transportation systems. Our demonstration videos, codes and datasets are available at the anonymous URL, https://anonymous.4open.science/r/OverFlowLight-FBF9.

*James Pritts,Felix Seegräber,Kevin Köser*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RANSAC变体依赖用户提供的内点尺度参数（阈值），该参数需从受污染数据中估计，且对算法性能影响显著。作者希望消除这一人为依赖性。

Method: 逆转传统推断顺序：先对固定内点分区下的内点尺度进行解析边缘化（共轭逆伽马先验），再优化分区。评分函数为封闭形式，涵盖非信息Jeffreys先验和信息性经验贝叶斯先验，支持O(N log N)的排序扫描计算。

Result: 在近7万图像对上，评分在阈值误校准时保持稳定（基线方法退化）；最少仅需2个验证对即可达到近最优精度（基线需~100倍更多数据）；验证数据稀缺时自动收紧先验正则化。

Conclusion: 首次实现了内点尺度完全不出现在公式中的RANSAC评分，在数据丰富和稀缺场景下均自适应，大幅降低了用户调参负担。

Abstract: The most widely used RANSAC variants score candidate models by counting inliers or summing per-point scores that saturate beyond a residual threshold. Every such score requires a user-supplied parameter that is a function of the inlier scale, which must itself be estimated from contaminated data. We remove this dependence by reversing the usual order of inference: rather than estimating the scale and then scoring against it, we marginalize the inlier scale analytically in closed form under a conjugate Inverse-Gamma prior for a fixed inlier partition, then optimize over partitions. A single closed-form expression spans the non-informative Jeffreys limit and informative empirical-Bayes priors, so the same score adapts across data-rich and data-scarce regimes without any change to the algorithm. The proposed RANSAC score is the first in which the inlier scale is genuinely absent from the formula. The score admits O(N log N ) computation via sort-and-sweep. On a benchmark of nearly 70 000 image pairs spanning different two-view estimation problems and both engineered and learned feature pipelines, the proposed score exceeds the state of the art (RANSAC, MSAC, GaU, MAGSAC): it stays nearly flat under threshold miscalibration where baselines degrade, reaches near-optimal accuracy from as few as two validation pairs where baselines need ont he order of 100 times more,. and tightens its prior regularization as validation data grows scarce.

Abstract: Byzantine-robust federated learning seeks to protect distributed model training from malicious or corrupted clients without requiring access to their private data. We further show that this two-level architecture can simultaneously address distribution mismatch in trust estimation and client drift across groups by combining local trust-based aggregation with heterogeneity-aware global optimizers such as FedAdam and SCAFFOLD. ### [40] [Learning in Markovian bandits with non-observable states and constrained decision epochs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27448)
*Thomas Hira,Victor Boone,Urtzi Ayesta,Ina Maria Verloop*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究马尔可夫强盗问题中状态不可观测且决策时刻可能受限时的遗憾最小化。引入“自退化马尔可夫强盗”推广，证明无先验知识时极少切换臂的算法遗憾必超对数级，但设计出近乎对数遗憾的UCB-NOM算法；给定先验知识则可达对数遗憾和√T对数级最坏情况界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出自退化马尔可夫强盗模型（rested Markovian bandits的推广），设计基于乐观原则的UCB-NOM算法。理论上先证明无先验知识时低频切换算法的遗憾下界ω(log T)，再给出UCB-NOM的遗憾上界分析。

Result: 无先验知识时，任意低频切换算法的遗憾必超对数级；UCB-NOM实现近乎对数遗憾。给定偏置函数界作为先验知识时，UCB-NOM达到O(log T)遗憾和O(√T log T)最坏情况遗憾。所有界均不依赖于马尔可夫链的状态数。

Conclusion: 在自退化马尔可夫强盗中，状态不可观测性仅带来“轻微不便”——虽无法严格达到对数遗憾，但近乎对数的遗憾是可行的；且若掌握一定先验知识，对数遗憾仍可实现。

Abstract: This paper studies the problem of regret minimization in Markovian bandits with \emph{non-observable states} and possibly \emph{constrained} decision epochs. The focus is restricted to a ``pure'' regret benchmark, that compares the performance of the learning algorithm to the best \emph{pure policy} which -- akin to optimal policies of stochastic bandits -- picks the optimal arm from start to finish without ever switching. We introduce a generalization of rested Markovian bandits, \emph{self-degrading Markovian bandits}, for which pure policies are always asymptotically optimal.We show that without prior knowledge on the underlying bandit, the regret of algorithms that switch arms rarely necessarily scales super-logarithmically for every bandit, i.e., as $ω(\log(T))$, where $T$ is the learning horizon. Despite the unreachability of the logarithmic regime, we design UCB-NOM, an optimistic algorithm inspired by UCB, of which the regret is nearly logarithmic. Lastly, we show that given prior knowledge on the Markovian bandit in the form of a bound on the bias functions of its arm, a proper instantiation of UCB-NOM achieves $O(\log(T))$ regret. We further show that this prior knowledge allows for a $O(\sqrt{T \log(T)})$ worst-case regret bound for UCB-NOM. Notably, our regret bounds do not depend on the number of states of the underlying Markov chains. Our findings suggest that the non-observability of states is a mild inconvenience in self-degrading Markovian bandits.

We consider Masked Diffusion Model (MDM) and introduce MDM-VGB, a discrete diffusion sampler that augments unmasking generation with theoretically principled reward-guided remasking. Inspired by the recent success of the classical Jerrum-Sinclair backtracking Markov chain in reward-tilted generation, MDM-VGB extends the backtracking random walk from a fixed prefix tree to a masked-state graph, allowing tokens to be unmasked and remasked at arbitrary positions. The resulting sampler favors unmasking and remasking moves that lead to higher-value partial configurations, enabling both effective high-reward generation and efficient repair of low-reward samples. We prove that MDM-VGB is robust to process-verifier noise and achieves quadratic complexity, while popular test-time heuristics such as best-of-$N$ can incur exponential complexity due to error accumulation. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多头注意力在所有层均匀分配head维度（dh = dmodel/h），导致早期层因维度受限无法捕捉复杂的高维上下文模式，形成结构性瓶颈。

Method: 提出Prism Transformer，采用渐进式head调度：随层数增加单调增加head数量，早期层用少而宽的head捕获局部组合模式，深层用多而窄的head分解为专门化的语言特征。该方法参数中性、计算中性，无额外训练/推理开销。

Abstract: Multi-head attention conventionally partitions the hidden dimension equally across all heads at every layer, enforcing an identical representational subspace dimension (dh = dmodel/h) throughout the models depth. In this work, we identify this uniform allocation as a fundamental structural bottleneck: due to their restricted dimensional space, early-layer heads are unable to faithfully capture complex, high-dimensional contextual patterns. To resolve this, we introduce the Prism Transformer, a novel architectural paradigm that replaces the static, uniform head configuration with a progressive head schedule. By monotonically increasing the head count across layers, the Prism Transformer naturally establishes a local-to-global representational hierarchy: early layers leverage fewer, exceptionally wide heads to capture complex, local compositional patterns, while deep layers deploy many, narrow heads to decompose these patterns into specialized linguistic features. Crucially, this structural shift is parameter-neutral, compute-neutral, and introduces zero training or inference overhead, preserving identical weight matrices and FLOP budgets as the standard Transformer. Across three model scales (124M, 354M, and 757M), the Prism Transformer consistently outperforms uniform baselines, achieving consistent reductions in validation loss alongside consistent gains on downstream zero-shot benchmarks (including PIQA, HellaSwag, ARC-Easy, and WinoGrande). Our findings demonstrate that non-uniform subspace allocation unlocks latent capacity within the standard Transformer budget, enabling more effective use of model capacity.

<details>

Abstract: We consider the cubic nonlinear Schrödinger (NLS) equation on two-dimensional flat tori with varying aspect ratios. In this formulation, the choice of aspect ratio governs the Fourier resonance structure, so rational and irrational geometries can exhibit different high-frequency cascade behaviors. We present a geometry-conditioned Fourier neural operator (FNO) for the cubic defocusing NLS equation, where the input consists of the real and imaginary parts of the solution together with the aspect-ratio parameter \(ω^2\). The model is trained to approximate the one-step solution operator and is evaluated on unseen trajectories generated from random-phase initial data using Fourier pseudospectral method. Our numerical experiments show that the learned operator captures the main solution dynamics on both tori and reproduces the distinct Sobolev norm behavior of the two geometries, with stronger \(H^2\)-growth on the rational torus and more constrained behavior on the irrational torus, consistent with the findings of \cite{hrabski2021energy}. We perform ablation studies to examine the roles of retained Fourier modes, activation functions, Fourier-layer depth, and explicit geometry conditioning. The results indicate that including $ω^2$ improves long-time predictive accuracy, especially for the rational geometry, and supports the use of geometry-aware neural operators for learning spectral-transfer phenomena in nonlinear dispersive partial differential equations.

### [44] [The Curse of Multiple Mediators: Hidden Interaction Effects in Activation Patching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27510)
*Sankaran Vaidyanathan,David Arbour,Aaron Mueller,Scott Niekum,David Jensen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文重新推导了激活修补（activation patching）的因果中介分析基础，发现其自然间接效应（NIE）估计量实际上包含了交互效应（INT），这些效应衡量组件因果作用对其他组件状态的依赖。作者证明INT无法被简单消除，且其规模随着clean与patched激活距离增大而增大，在模型局部仿射时趋于零。INT并非噪声，而是揭示因果结论是否依赖提示（prompt）的诊断工具，以及基于NIE的贪心组件排序会遗漏仅能通过组合搜索发现的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机械可解释性中广泛使用激活修补（activation patching）来衡量模型组件的因果重要性，但该方法在因果中介分析框架下的严格数学基础尚未被充分检验，使得潜在的估计偏差（即NIE中混杂的交互效应）被忽视，可能导致错误的因果归因结论。

Method: 从因果中介分析重新推导激活修补的NIE估计量，揭示其包含交互效应（INT）；通过理论分析证明INT的性质（随激活距离增大、局部仿射时消失、可组合分解为高阶交互）；在GPT-2的IOI电路上进行实证验证，展示INT导致的组件可见性偏差和 faithfulness 分数不稳定问题。

Result: 证明了激活修补的NIE估计量必然包含交互效应INT；INT在GPT-2 IOI电路中导致条件重要的组件要么不可见要么被夸大；INT方差解释了faithfulness分数的已知不稳定性；INT随clean与patched激活距离线性增长；INT可分解为高阶交互作用。

Conclusion: 交互效应INT不是可以或应该被消除的噪声，而是有用的诊断工具：其幅度和符号可指示因果结论是否依赖于特定提示，以及基于NIE的贪心排序会遗漏需要组合搜索才能发现的机制。研究者应正视INT的存在，将其作为理解模型行为的额外信息源。

Abstract: Activation patching is the primary tool in mechanistic interpretability. It attributes causal responsibility for a model behavior to each of its individual components by estimating its natural indirect effect (NIE). Re-deriving the activation patching estimand from causal mediation analysis, we find that the NIE does not solely capture the causal effect through the specific component. It also contains interaction effects (INT) that measure how much the component's causal effect itself depends on the state of other components in the model. A natural response may be to try to eliminate INT by adjusting the estimator or unit of analysis, but each of these potential remedies has predictable failure modes. We demonstrate these failure modes in the GPT-2 IOI circuit; components whose causal importance is conditional on the state of other components are either invisible or artificially inflated, and INT variance explains the previously documented instability of faithfulness scores. We prove that INT scales with the distance between clean and patched component activations, is negligible when the model is locally affine, and decomposes combinatorially into pairwise and higher-order group interactions. Despite its inevitability, INT is not a nuisance to be eliminated, but rather a diagnostic for interpretability studies. Its individual and group-level magnitude and sign signal when causal conclusions are prompt-dependent, and when greedy NIE-based component ranking will miss mechanisms only discoverable through combinatorial search.

</details>


### [45] [Towards Value-Constrained Credit Assignment in Fully Delegated AI Cooperatives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28217)
*Young Yoon,Jimin Kim,Soyeon Park*

TL;DR: 提出一个在全委托AI合作社中基于价值筛选的奖励分配框架，利用遍历学习（TL）实现细粒度贡献归因，优于传统联邦学习。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习（如FedAvg）在贡献归因上粒度不够细，且数据估值和联邦贡献估计方法难以处理异构价值约束下的奖励分配问题。

Method: 提出了价值条件梯度过滤、在线边际贡献信号和累计收益结算机制，在遍历学习（TL）框架下实现去中心化反向传播，保留清晰的遍历路径和梯度路径。

Result: TL相比FedAvg风格的联邦学习能提供更细粒度的归因，且不会出现聚合中心化分布式学习的质量损失。

Conclusion: 该框架为异构价值约束下的AI合作贡献分配提供了新思路，并在数据估值、联邦贡献估计、个性化联邦学习和多元对齐等多个方向具有参考意义。

The key idea is to credit only those updates that remain admissible after screening them against each principal's value profile. We formulate value-conditioned gradient filtering, online marginal contribution signals, and cumulative revenue settlement within a traversal learning (TL) substrate. TL is especially attractive here because it performs decentralized backpropagation without the quality loss associated with aggregation-centric distributed learning and, we argue, offers a finer attribution substrate than FedAvg-style federated learning by preserving explicit traversal and gradient paths. The framework is positioned against data valuation, federated contribution estimation, personalized federated learning, and pluralistic alignment.

### [46] [Boundary condition fidelity for bottom-hole pressure and CO2 plume prediction in geological carbon storage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27515)
*Romal Ramadhan,Seyyed A. Hosseini,Larry W. Lake*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了碳封存模拟中截断域边界条件对井底压力和CO2羽流预测的影响，发现保留角落孔隙体积是关键，渐进修正法+传导率校正最稳定（BHP NRMSE<3.7%，羽流IoU>0.97）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际地质碳封存模拟常使用截断域以降低计算成本，但人工边界会扭曲压力扩散和CO2饱和度分布，导致预测不准确。现有研究对边界处理方法的系统性对比不足，需量化不同边界条件对关键预测指标的影响。

Method: 在均质和非均质储层中，对比10种截断域边界处理方法（均匀孔隙体积乘数、传导率修饰、角落孔隙体积校正、分层校正、渐进修正等）与全域参考模拟，使用BHP RMSE/NRMSE、峰值压力偏差和羽流IoU作为评价指标。

Conclusion: 角落孔隙体积的保真是截断域建模最重要的前提；传导率校正需根据储层非均质性谨慎应用；渐进修正法具有最佳的跨场景鲁棒性。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of bottom-hole pressure (BHP) and CO2 plume migration is essential for safe geological carbon storage, yet practical simulations often rely on truncated domains where artificial boundaries distort pressure diffusion and CO2 saturation footprints. In this study, we evaluate how boundary-condition fidelity affects BHP and CO2 plume prediction by comparing ten reduced-domain boundary treatments against full-domain reference simulations in homogeneous and heterogeneous reservoirs. We test uniform pore-volume multipliers, transmissibility modifiers, corner-adjusted pore-volume corrections, layered corrections, and gradual modifiers using BHP RMSE, NRMSE, peak pressure deviation, and plume Intersection over Union (IoU) as performance metrics. Our results show that conserving corner pore volume is the most important requirement for truncated-domain modeling. We find that uniform treatments which neglect corner storage generate large pressure errors, with BHP RMSE of 362 to 382 psi in the homogeneous model and 250 to 304 psi in the heterogeneous model, and yield plume IoU values near 0.80 to 0.84, indicating roughly 16 to 20% of the combined plume area is misrepresented. Corner-adjusted scenarios substantially reduce pressure errors and raise plume IoU above 0.94, but we observe that transmissibility correction is not universally beneficial. In homogeneous reservoirs, uniform transmissibility adjustment improves pressure fidelity; in heterogeneous reservoirs, it can over-restrict flow across variable-permeability boundary faces, increasing BHP error and contracting the predicted plume. We find the gradual modifier with transmissibility correction provides the most consistent performance, achieving BHP NRMSE below 3.7% and plume IoU above 0.97 in both reservoir types.

*Arnav Raj*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PEBS是一种基于经验贝叶斯收缩的逐标注者仿射校准方法，用于RLHF奖励建模，能在不重训练奖励模型的情况下，显著降低个体标注者的预测误差（RMSE降低8.58%-9.66%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLHF奖励模型将所有标注者的偏好数据混合在一起，拟合一个全局的仿射校准器，忽略了个体标注者在评分偏移和斜率上的系统性差异，导致模型不能准确反映任何单个标注者的真实偏好。

Method: PEBS为每位标注者分别拟合仿射校准器，利用其标注数据的保留部分，然后应用Morris-James-Stein经验贝叶斯收缩向总体均值靠拢，整个过程以闭式形式完成，无需重新训练奖励模型。

Abstract: Reward models for Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) pool preferences across thousands of annotators and fit one global affine calibrator, collapsing raters with systematically different rating-scale offsets and slopes into a single average-rater fit that does not match any individual annotator. PEBS is a per-rater empirical-Bayes shrinkage estimator: it fits per-rater affine calibrators on a held-out slice of each annotator's ratings and applies Morris-James-Stein empirical-Bayes shrinkage toward the population mean, in closed form and without retraining the reward model. On PRISM, PEBS reduces within-user held-out RMSE by 8.58% over the pooled population-slope baseline. The procedure replicates on PluriHarms harm ratings (Qwen-2.5 base, in-family) with a +9.66% RMSE reduction over the same population-slope baseline. PEBS is a closed-form post-hoc estimator for annotator-specific affine calibration in RLHF reward modeling; it leaves the reward base model unchanged and estimates only the rater-level map used at inference time for new ratings.
